msg:Environment: The location of the hotel is good. It is on the edge of the core area of Puyang City. It is very convenient to drive by car.

Service: The waiters need further training, the service awareness is not strong enough, the room attendants greeted very warmly, and the waiters in the breakfast area were not professional enough.

Sanitation: Because the bed in the executive room is relatively large, this time I chose a slightly more expensive executive room, but after I checked in, I felt as if no one lived there for a long time. I should have done a good job of hygiene before, but it was a little dusty.

Small suggestion: It has been mentioned in the hotel's feedback call that the breakfast time is 6:30-9:30. However, half of the lights were turned off at 9:30 on the day we dined, and there were still many guests dining at that time. Because Arcadia is originally a resort hotel, it is normal for guests to wake up late. It is recommended to extend the breakfast time to 10:00. Even if it cannot be extended, don’t turn off the lights at once. This feels like driving away guests. Star hotels should not have such a sense of experience, I hope to improve.

卡地亞酒店給我留下很好印象。
